2015-08-11 16:13:10.4642 | INFO | addGameData:
declare @webid nvarchar(50)
declare @allianceid int,@teamaid int ,@teambid int
begin
set @webid=null
select @webid=webid from [IceHockeySchedules] with(nolock) where webid='6DTR1ZCo' AND GameType='IHBF'
if @webid is null
begin
select @allianceid=allianceid from [IceHockeyAlliance] with(nolock) where alliancename='WORLD: Club Friendly' and gametype='IHBF'
SELECT @teamaid=teamid FROM [IceHockeyTeam] WITH (NOLOCK) WHERE TeamName='Metallurg Novokuznetsk (Rus)' and gametype='IHBF'
SELECT @teambid=teamid FROM [IceHockeyTeam] WITH (NOLOCK) WHERE TeamName='Vladivostok (Rus)' and gametype='IHBF'
INSERT INTO [IceHockeySchedules] ([AllianceID],[GameDate],[GameTime],[GameStates],[TeamAID],[TeamBID],[RunsA],[RunsB],[RA],[RB],[WebID],[TrackerText],[StatusText],[GameType],[Display]) VALUES (@allianceid,'2015-08-10','16:00','E',@teamaid,@teambid,'0,1,0','1,0,1','1','2','6DTR1ZCo','','結束','IHBF',0)
end
end

2015-08-11 16:14:13.7284 | INFO | addGameData:
declare @webid nvarchar(50)
declare @allianceid int,@teamaid int ,@teambid int
begin
set @webid=null
select @webid=webid from [IceHockeySchedules] with(nolock) where webid='6DTR1ZCo' AND GameType='IHBF'
if @webid is null
begin
select @allianceid=allianceid from [IceHockeyAlliance] with(nolock) where alliancename='WORLD: Club Friendly' and gametype='IHBF'
SELECT @teamaid=teamid FROM [IceHockeyTeam] WITH (NOLOCK) WHERE TeamName='Metallurg Novokuznetsk (Rus)' and gametype='IHBF'
SELECT @teambid=teamid FROM [IceHockeyTeam] WITH (NOLOCK) WHERE TeamName='Vladivostok (Rus)' and gametype='IHBF'
INSERT INTO [IceHockeySchedules] ([AllianceID],[GameDate],[GameTime],[GameStates],[TeamAID],[TeamBID],[RunsA],[RunsB],[RA],[RB],[WebID],[TrackerText],[StatusText],[GameType],[Display]) VALUES (@allianceid,'2015-08-10','16:00','E',@teamaid,@teambid,'0,1,0','1,0,1','1','2','6DTR1ZCo','','結束','IHBF',0)
end
end
